***guile.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:guile.html>guile</a> (38239)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">gile</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">gile</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:guile.html>guile</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">deception</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*wigila</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">ruse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> Proto-Germanic with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wile</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:guile.html>guile</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">guiles</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Astuteness often marked by a certain sense of cunning or artful deception.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> April 24,  <a href = vnd.unilang:phil.html>Phil</a> Dawkes,  âBarcelona 2-2 Chelseaâ, in  <cite>BBC Sport</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/sport/0/football/17817584">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a result that owed a lot to a <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:guile.html>guile</a></b> from Ramires but more to a display of <a href = vnd.unilang:guts.html>guts</a> from the Brazilian and his team-mates after <a href = vnd.unilang:terry.html>Terry</a>'s needless dismissal eight minutes before half-time for driving a knee into the back of Alexis Sanchez off the ball.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> November 11,  <a href = vnd.unilang:rory.html>Rory</a> Houston,  âEstonia 0-4 Republic of Irelandâ, in  <cite>RTE Sport</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.rte.ie/sport/soccer/2011/1111/estonia_ireland_report.html">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Estonia <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> struggling to get to <a href = vnd.unilang:grips.html>grips</a> with the game while Ireland <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> showing a composure and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:guile.html>guile</a></b> that demonstrated their experience in <a href = vnd.unilang:play-off.html>play-off</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ties.html>ties</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Deceptiveness, deceit, fraud, duplicity, dishonesty.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1611</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">The Holy Bible,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Conteyning the Old Testament, and the New. ***gunnen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a> (9642)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*giunnan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gaunnanÄ</i>, a prefixed form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*unnanÄ</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">gÃ¶nnen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with indirect object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to think someone deserves something, to witness or acknowledge someone's success or enjoyment without envy or grudge <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually referring to positive outcomes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>2012</b>, Natasja Oosterloo, <i>Twitter <a href = vnd.unilang:jezelf.html>jezelf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:baan.html>baan</a></i>, page 37.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> gunfactor <a href = vnd.unilang:zorgt.html>zorgt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ervoor.html>ervoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:positief.html>positief</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:denken.html>denken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daardoor.html>daardoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Likeability ensures that people think positively about you and because of that they <b>will be <a href = vnd.unilang:okay.html>okay</a> with</b> you <b>getting</b> something <b>nice</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gegund.html>gegund</a></b>!</i> â <span class="e-translation">You really <b>deserved</b> it!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gunt.html>gunt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:functie.html>functie</a>.</i> â <span class="e-translation">He <b>thinks</b> you <b>deserved</b> that position.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">misgunnen</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with indirect object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to award, to grant <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of <a href = vnd.unilang:orders.html>orders</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:tenders.html>tenders</a>, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>2005</b>, <i>Aanbestedingsreglement <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> 2005: ARW 2005</i>, page 201.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> aanbesteder <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verplicht.html>verplicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opdracht.html>opdracht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The contracting party <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not required to <b>grant</b> the order.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestuur.html>bestuur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:besprak.html>besprak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opdracht.html>opdracht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The managing board <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> discussing to whom they would <b>award</b> the order.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with indirect object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give, usually out of benevolence or <a href = vnd.unilang:grace.html>grace</a>; to grant

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gunst.html>gunst</a> (2749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunst.html>gunst</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gonst.html>gonst</a></i>, prefixed from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ge-</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">onst</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">onste</i>, the latter from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">anst</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*unstiz</i>.
Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gunnen.html>gunnen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-st</i>.

<p>Unknown. Possibly from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gurney.html>Gurney</a> cab</i>, a type of horse-drawn cab on <a href = vnd.unilang:wheels.html>wheels</a> named after Theodore <a href = vnd.unilang:gurney.html>Gurney</a>, the US inventor credited with creating and patenting it in about 1883.

***gyro.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gyro.html>gyro</a> (82971)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally a shortening of gyroscope.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gyro.html>gyro</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gyros</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A gyroscope</li>
<li>A gyrocompass</li>
<li>An autogyro</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">Î³ÏÏÎ¿Ï</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gÃ½ros</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; from the turning of the meat on a spit. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gyre</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gyrus.html>gyrus</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gyro.html>gyro</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gyros</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A style of Greek sandwich commonly filled with grilled meat, tomato, onions, and tzatziki sauce.
<dl><dd><i>I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> have a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gyro.html>gyro</a></b>, please.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The correct pronunciation of this word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> disputed. The pronunciation <span class="IPA">/ËdÊaÉªÉ¹oÊ/</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often proscribed. All of the listed pronunciations may be found in use. (The modern Greek pronunciation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <span class="IPA">/ËÊiÉ¾os/</span>.):

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hÄge</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">haghe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hago</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*hagÅ</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hagÃ´</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">hedge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kaghon</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haag.html>haag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hagen.html>hagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haag.html>haagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A hedge, thicket of <a href = vnd.unilang:woody.html>woody</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bushes.html>bushes</a> planted in a row</li>
<li>A lane, (often double) row of lined-up persons or <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a>, as for a formal guard of honor inspection</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Undergrowth, a dense low forest</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">haeye</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hÃ¡-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">shark</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the /j/ appearing influenced by the declined forms /hajÉ(n)/. Probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hanh-u-</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">haj</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hai.html>Hai</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Caribbean_reef_shark.jpg/250px-Caribbean_reef_shark.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="156" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Caribbean_reef_shark.jpg/375px-Caribbean_reef_shark.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Caribbean_reef_shark.jpg/500px-Caribbean_reef_shark.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1968" data-file-height="1228" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i>Caribische rifhaai</i><br />Caribbean Reef Shark</div></div></div>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">haer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiro.html>hiro</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hezÅi</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_3">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></strong> (<i>dependent possessive, independent possive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hare.html>hare</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Third-person plural possessive adjective: their</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>Haar</a></i> (âtheirâ) <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the normal Middle Dutch form for all genders in the plural. In modern Dutch, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i> successively replaced <i><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i> in this function. Some writers of the 19th and early 20th century made a learned distinction, using <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i> as the masculine and neuter plural, but <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i> for the feminine in both singular and plural: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hunne.html>hunne</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwen.html>vrouwen</a></i> (âmen and their wivesâ) versus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwen.html>vrouwen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hare.html>hare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a></i> (âwomen and their husbandsâ).</li></ul>

***haarspeldbocht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:haarspeldbocht.html>haarspeldbocht</a> (117031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haarspeld.html>haarspeld</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bocht.html>bocht</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hairpin turn</i>; in the oldest use referring to a turn by an aeroplane.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haarspeldbocht.html>haarspeldbocht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haarspeldbochten.html>haarspeldbochten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A hairpin bend, a hairpin turn. <span class="defdate">[from early 20th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1909</b> September 3, J. <a href = vnd.unilang:hurst.html>Hurst</a> Hayes, "<a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> aeroplaan <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> liefdesgeschiedenis <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toekomst.html>toekomst</a>", tr. from English (original title "An Aeroplane for Two. A Love Romance of the Future"), <i>Middelburgsche <a href = vnd.unilang:courant.html>Courant</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>Vol</a>. 152, No. 207, page 1.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedwingen.html>bedwingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geestdrift.html>geestdrift</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegenover.html>tegenover</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezellin.html>gezellin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spreken.html>spreken</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>juist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nadat.html>nadat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijzonder.html>bijzonder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:scherpe.html>scherpe</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haarspeldbocht.html>haarspeldbocht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemaakt.html>gemaakt</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I couldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> help speaking my enthusiasm to my companion after I <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> just made a particularly sharp <b>hairpin turn</b>. <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">original English</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hachtelijk</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hacht</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>precarious, insecure, dangerous</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
